বিস্তারিত প্রজেক্ট বিবরণ (প্রথম ৫০টি)
Beginner Level (১-৫০)
প্রজেক্ট ১: ক্যালকুলেটর
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>ক্যালকুলেটর</title>
    <style>
        .calculator {
            width: 300px;
            margin: 50px auto;
            padding: 20px;
            border: 1px solid #ccc;
            border-radius: 10px;
            box-shadow: 0 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);
        }
        .display {
            width: 100%;
            height: 60px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            padding: 10px;
            font-size: 24px;
            text-align: right;
            border: 1px solid #ccc;
            border-radius: 5px;
        }
        .buttons {
            display: grid;
            grid-template-columns: repeat(4, 1fr);
            gap: 10px;
        }
        button {
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 18px;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 5px;
            background-color: #f0f0f0;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        button:hover {
            background-color: #e0e0e0;
        }
        .operator {
            background-color: #ff9500;
            color: white;
        }
        .equals {
            background-color: #28a745;
            color: white;
        }
        .clear {
            background-color: #dc3545;
            color: white;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="calculator">
        <input type="text" class="display" id="display" readonly>
        <div class="buttons">
            <button onclick="clearDisplay()" class="clear">C</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('/')">/</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('*')">×</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('-')">-</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('7')">7</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('8')">8</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('9')">9</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('+')" class="operator">+</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('4')">4</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('5')">5</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('6')">6</button>
            <button onclick="calculate()" class="equals" rowspan="2">=</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('1')">1</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('2')">2</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('3')">3</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('0')" colspan="2">0</button>
            <button onclick="appendToDisplay('.')">.</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function appendToDisplay(value) {
            document.getElementById('display').value += value;
        }
        
        function clearDisplay() {
            document.getElementById('display').value = '';
        }
        
        function calculate() {
            try {
                const result = eval(document.getElementById('display').value);
                document.getElementById('display').value = result;
            } catch (error) {
                alert('ভুল ইনপুট');
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ২: ডিজিটাল ঘড়ি
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>ডিজিটাল ঘড়ি</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
            height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .clock {
            background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
            backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
        }
        .time {
            font-size: 80px;
            color: white;
            text-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(255,255,255,0.5);
            letter-spacing: 5px;
        }
        .date {
            font-size: 30px;
            color: white;
            text-align: center;
            margin-top: 20px;
            opacity: 0.9;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="clock">
        <div class="time" id="time">00:00:00</div>
        <div class="date" id="date">সোমবার, ১ জানুয়ারি ২০২৪</div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function updateClock() {
            const now = new Date();
            
            // সময়
            const hours = now.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0');
            const minutes = now.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0');
            const seconds = now.getSeconds().toString().padStart(2, '0');
            document.getElementById('time').textContent = `${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}`;
            
            // তারিখ
            const days = ['রবিবার', 'সোমবার', 'মঙ্গলবার', 'বুধবার', 'বৃহস্পতিবার', 'শুক্রবার', 'শনিবার'];
            const months = ['জানুয়ারি', 'ফেব্রুয়ারি', 'মার্চ', 'এপ্রিল', 'মে', 'জুন', 'জুলাই', 'আগস্ট', 'সেপ্টেম্বর', 'অক্টোবর', 'নভেম্বর', 'ডিসেম্বর'];
            
            const day = days[now.getDay()];
            const date = now.getDate();
            const month = months[now.getMonth()];
            const year = now.getFullYear();
            
            document.getElementById('date').textContent = `${day}, ${date} ${month} ${year}`;
        }
        
        setInterval(updateClock, 1000);
        updateClock();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৩: টো-ডু লিস্ট
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>টো-ডু লিস্ট</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff6b6b 0%, #ff8e8e 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;

        }
        .container {
            max-width: 600px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            background: white;

            padding: 30px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        }
        h1 {
            text-align: center;
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        .input-section {
            display: flex;
            gap: 10px;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        #taskInput {
            flex: 1;
            padding: 15px;

        }
        #addTask {

        #addTask:hover {

        @keyframes slideIn {

        .task.completed {

        .stats {

        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>📝 আমার টো-ডু লিস্ট</h1>
        
        <div class="input-section">
            <input type="text" id="taskInput" placeholder="নতুন টাস্ক লিখুন...">
            <button id="addTask">যোগ করুন</button>
        </div>
        
        <div id="taskList"></div>
        
        <div class="stats">
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-value" id="totalTasks">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">মোট টাস্ক</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-value" id="completedTasks">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">সম্পন্ন</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-value" id="pendingTasks">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">বাকি</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let tasks = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('tasks')) || [];
        
        function renderTasks() {
            const taskList = document.getElementById('taskList');
            taskList.innerHTML = '';
            
            tasks.forEach((task, index) => {
                const taskElement = document.createElement('div');
                taskElement.className = `task ${task.completed ? 'completed' : ''}`;
                
                taskElement.innerHTML = `
                    <span class="task-text">${task.text}</span>
                    <div class="task-actions">
                        <button class="complete-btn" onclick="toggleComplete(${index})">✓</button>
                        <button class="delete-btn" onclick="deleteTask(${index})">🗑️</button>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                taskList.appendChild(taskElement);
            });
            
            updateStats();
            saveTasks();
        }
        
        function addTask() {
            const input = document.getElementById('taskInput');
            const text = input.value.trim();
            
            if (text) {
                tasks.push({ text, completed: false });
                input.value = '';
                renderTasks();
            }
        }
        
        function toggleComplete(index) {
            tasks[index].completed = !tasks[index].completed;
            renderTasks();
        }
        
        function deleteTask(index) {
            tasks.splice(index, 1);
            renderTasks();
        }
        
        function updateStats() {
            const total = tasks.length;
            const completed = tasks.filter(task => task.completed).length;
            const pending = total - completed;
            
            document.getElementById('totalTasks').textContent = total;
            document.getElementById('completedTasks').textContent = completed;
            document.getElementById('pendingTasks').textContent = pending;
        }
        
        function saveTasks() {
            localStorage.setItem('tasks', JSON.stringify(tasks));
        }
        
        document.getElementById('addTask').addEventListener('click', addTask);
        document.getElementById('taskInput').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') addTask();
        });
        
        renderTasks();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৪: রঙ পরিবর্তনকারী

    <script>
        const body = document.body;
        const colorCode = document.getElementById('colorCode');
        
        function getRandomColor() {
            const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';
            let color = '#';
            for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
                color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];
            }
            return color;
        }
        
        function setColor(color) {
            body.style.backgroundColor = color;
            colorCode.textContent = color;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('randomBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            const color = getRandomColor();
            setColor(color);
        });
        
        document.getElementById('copyBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(colorCode.textContent).then(() => {
                alert('রঙ কপি হয়েছে!');
            });
        });
        
        document.getElementById('resetBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
            setColor('#667eea');
        });
        
        setColor('#667eea');
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৫: কাউন্টডাউন টাইমার
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>কাউন্টডাউন টাইমার</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff6b6b 0%, #ff8e8e 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            text-align: center;
        }
        h1 {
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        .timer-display {
            font-size: 80px;
            font-weight: bold;
            color: #ff6b6b;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
            font-family: monospace;
        }
        .input-section {
            display: flex;
            gap: 10px;
            justify-content: center;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        input {
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 18px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 10px;
            width: 100px;
            text-align: center;
        }
        .buttons {
            display: flex;
            gap: 15px;
            justify-content: center;
        }
        button {
            padding: 15px 30px;
            font-size: 16px;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 10px;
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        #startBtn {
            background: #4caf50;
            color: white;
        }
        #pauseBtn {
            background: #ff9800;
            color: white;
        }
        #resetBtn {
            background: #f44336;
            color: white;
        }
        button:hover {
            transform: translateY(-2px);
            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        }
        button:disabled {
            opacity: 0.5;
            cursor: not-allowed;
            transform: none;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>⏰ কাউন্টডাউন টাইমার</h1>
        
        <div class="timer-display" id="timer">00:00:00</div>
        
        <div class="input-section">
            <input type="number" id="hours" placeholder="ঘণ্টা" min="0" value="0">
            <input type="number" id="minutes" placeholder="মিনিট" min="0" value="0">
            <input type="number" id="seconds" placeholder="সেকেন্ড" min="0" value="30">
        </div>
        
        <div class="buttons">
            <button id="startBtn">শুরু করুন</button>
            <button id="pauseBtn" disabled>বিরতি</button>
            <button id="resetBtn">রিসেট</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let timerInterval;
        let timeLeft = 0;
        let isPaused = false;
        
        const timerDisplay = document.getElementById('timer');
        const hoursInput = document.getElementById('hours');
        const minutesInput = document.getElementById('minutes');
        const secondsInput = document.getElementById('seconds');
        const startBtn = document.getElementById('startBtn');
        const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('pauseBtn');
        const resetBtn = document.getElementById('resetBtn');
        
        function updateDisplay() {
            const hours = Math.floor(timeLeft / 3600);
            const minutes = Math.floor((timeLeft % 3600) / 60);
            const seconds = timeLeft % 60;
            
            timerDisplay.textContent = `${hours.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
        }
        
        function startTimer() {
            if (timeLeft === 0) {
                const hours = parseInt(hoursInput.value) || 0;
                const minutes = parseInt(minutesInput.value) || 0;
                const seconds = parseInt(secondsInput.value) || 0;
                
                timeLeft = hours * 3600 + minutes * 60 + seconds;
                
                if (timeLeft <= 0) {
                    alert('দয়া করে সময় দিন');
                    return;
                }
            }
            
            startBtn.disabled = true;
            pauseBtn.disabled = false;
            hoursInput.disabled = true;
            minutesInput.disabled = true;
            secondsInput.disabled = true;
            
            timerInterval = setInterval(() => {
                if (!isPaused) {
                    timeLeft--;
                    updateDisplay();
                    
                    if (timeLeft <= 0) {
                        clearInterval(timerInterval);
                        timerDisplay.textContent = '00:00:00';
                        startBtn.disabled = false;
                        pauseBtn.disabled = true;
                        hoursInput.disabled = false;
                        minutesInput.disabled = false;
                        secondsInput.disabled = false;
                        alert('সময় শেষ!');
                    }
                }
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        function pauseTimer() {
            isPaused = !isPaused;
            pauseBtn.textContent = isPaused ? 'চালু করুন' : 'বিরতি';
        }
        
        function resetTimer() {
            clearInterval(timerInterval);
            timeLeft = 0;
            isPaused = false;
            updateDisplay();
            
            startBtn.disabled = false;
            pauseBtn.disabled = true;
            pauseBtn.textContent = 'বিরতি';
            hoursInput.disabled = false;
            minutesInput.disabled = false;
            secondsInput.disabled = false;
            
            hoursInput.value = '0';
            minutesInput.value = '0';
            secondsInput.value = '30';
        }
        
        startBtn.addEventListener('click', startTimer);
        pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', pauseTimer);
        resetBtn.addEventListener('click', resetTimer);
        
        updateDisplay();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>📜 র্যান্ডম কোট জেনারেটর</h1>
        
        <div class="quote-box">
            <div class="quote-text" id="quoteText">জীবন হলো যা ঘটে যখন আপনি অন্য পরিকল্পনা নিয়ে ব্যস্ত থাকেন।</div>
            <div class="quote-author" id="quoteAuthor">- জন লেনন</div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="buttons">
            <button id="newQuoteBtn">নতুন কোট</button>
            <button id="copyQuoteBtn">কপি করুন</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const quotes = [
            { text: "জীবন হলো যা ঘটে যখন আপনি অন্য পরিকল্পনা নিয়ে ব্যস্ত থাকেন।", author: "জন লেনন" },
            { text: "সফলতা চূড়ান্ত নয়, ব্যর্থতা মারাত্মক নয়: এটা হলো চলতে থাকার সাহস।", author: "উইনস্টন চার্চিল" },
            { text: "আপনার সময় সীমিত, তাই অন্য কারো জীবন যাপনে এটি নষ্ট করবেন না।", author: "স্টিভ জবস" },
            { text: "ভবিষ্যৎ ভবিষ্যদ্বাণী করার সবচেয়ে ভালো উপায় হলো এটি তৈরি করা।", author: "পিটার ড্রাকার" },
            { text: "বড় হওয়ার সাহস রাখুন, আপনার মনে ও আত্মায় পৌঁছানোর চেষ্টা করুন।", author: "অড্রে হেপবার্ন" },
            { text: "হাজার মাইলের যাত্রা শুরু হয় একটি পদক্ষেপ দিয়ে।", author: "লাও ত্ৎসে" },
            { text: "আপনি যা বিশ্বাস করেন তা যদি আপনি করতে পারেন, তবে আপনি যা স্বপ্ন দেখেন তা অর্জন করতে পারেন।", author: "বারবারা বুশ" },
            { text: "অন্ধকারকে অভিশাপ দেওয়ার চেয়ে একটি মোমবাতি জ্বালানো ভালো।", author: "কনফুসিয়াস" },
            { text: "জীবনের অর্থ হলো অর্থপূর্ণ জীবন যাপন করা।", author: "এরিস্টটল" },
            { text: "যা সম্ভব তা করতে গিয়ে অসম্ভবকে স্বপ্ন দেখুন।", author: "রবীন্দ্রনাথ ঠাকুর" }
        ];

        function getRandomQuote() {
            const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * quotes.length);
            return quotes[randomIndex];
        }

        function displayNewQuote() {
            const quote = getRandomQuote();
            document.getElementById('quoteText').textContent = quote.text;
            document.getElementById('quoteAuthor').textContent = `- ${quote.author}`;
        }

        function copyQuote() {
            const quote = document.getElementById('quoteText').textContent;
            const author = document.getElementById('quoteAuthor').textContent;
            const fullQuote = `${quote} ${author}`;
            
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullQuote).then(() => {
                alert('কোট কপি হয়েছে!');
            });
        }

        document.getElementById('newQuoteBtn').addEventListener('click', displayNewQuote);
        document.getElementById('copyQuoteBtn').addEventListener('click', copyQuote);
    </script>
</body>

প্রজেক্ট ৭: প্যালিনড্রোম চেকার

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>প্যালিনড্রোম চেকার</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff6b6b 0%, #ff8e8e 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            max-width: 500px;
            width: 90%;
            text-align: center;
        }
        h1 {
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        .description {
            color: #666;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
            font-size: 16px;
        }
        .input-group {
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        #textInput {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 18px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;

            box-sizing: border-box;
        }
        #checkBtn {

            font-size: 18px;
            background: #ff6b6b;
            color: white;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 10px;
            cursor: pointer;

        }

            transform: translateY(-2px);
            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(255,107,107,0.3);
        }
        .result {
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 10px;
            font-size: 24px;
            font-weight: bold;
            display: none;
        }
        .result.palindrome {
            background: #d4edda;
            color: #155724;
            display: block;
        }
        .result.not-palindrome {
            background: #f8d7da;
            color: #721c24;
            display: block;
        }
        .examples {
            margin-top: 30px;
            color: #666;
        }
        .example-tag {
            display: inline-block;
            background: #f0f0f0;
            padding: 5px 10px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            margin: 5px;
            font-size: 14px;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🔄 প্যালিনড্রোম চেকার</h1>
        <p class="description">যে শব্দ বা বাক্য উল্টো করে পড়লেও একই হয়, তাই প্যালিনড্রোম</p>
        
        <div class="input-group">
            <input type="text" id="textInput" placeholder="যেমন: radar, madam, 121">
            <button id="checkBtn">পরীক্ষা করুন</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="result" id="result"></div>
        
        <div class="examples">
            <p>উদাহরণ:</p>
            <span class="example-tag">radar</span>
            <span class="example-tag">madam</span>
            <span class="example-tag">121</span>
            <span class="example-tag">কাক</span>
            <span class="example-tag">না</span>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function isPalindrome(str) {
            // শুধু অক্ষর এবং সংখ্যা রাখি, বাকি সব বাদ দিই
            const cleaned = str.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9\u0980-\u09FF]/g, '');
            const reversed = cleaned.split('').reverse().join('');
            return cleaned === reversed;
        }

        function checkPalindrome() {
            const input = document.getElementById('textInput').value;
            const resultDiv = document.getElementById('result');
            
            if (input.trim() === '') {
                alert('দয়া করে কিছু লিখুন');
                return;
            }
            
            if (isPalindrome(input)) {
                resultDiv.textContent = `"${input}" একটি প্যালিনড্রোম!`;
                resultDiv.className = 'result palindrome';
            } else {
                resultDiv.textContent = `"${input}" একটি প্যালিনড্রোম নয়`;
                resultDiv.className = 'result not-palindrome';
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('checkBtn').addEventListener('click', checkPalindrome);
        document.getElementById('textInput').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') checkPalindrome();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৮: Vowel কাউন্টার
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Vowel কাউন্টার</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f093fb 0%, #f5576c 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            max-width: 600px;
            width: 90%;
        }
        h1 {
            text-align: center;
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        textarea {
            width: 100%;
            height: 150px;
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 18px;

        <textarea id="textInput" placeholder="আপনার টেক্সট লিখুন..."></textarea>
        
        <div class="stats">
            <div class="stat-card total">
                <div class="stat-value" id="totalChars">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">মোট অক্ষর</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card">
                <div class="stat-value" id="totalVowels">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">মোট Vowel</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card">
                <div class="stat-value" id="totalConsonants">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">মোট Consonant</div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="vowel-breakdown">
            <h3>Vowel এর বিবরণ</h3>
            <div class="vowel-grid">
                <div class="vowel-item">
                    <div class="vowel-letter">A/a</div>
                    <div class="vowel-count" id="countA">0</div>
                </div>
                <div class="vowel-item">
                    <div class="vowel-letter">E/e</div>
                    <div class="vowel-count" id="countE">0</div>
                </div>
                <div class="vowel-item">
                    <div class="vowel-letter">I/i</div>
                    <div class="vowel-count" id="countI">0</div>
                </div>
                <div class="vowel-item">
                    <div class="vowel-letter">O/o</div>
                    <div class="vowel-count" id="countO">0</div>
                </div>
                <div class="vowel-item">
                    <div class="vowel-letter">U/u</div>
                    <div class="vowel-count" id="countU">0</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function countVowels() {
            const text = document.getElementById('textInput').value;
            
            // মোট অক্ষর (শুধু অক্ষর এবং সংখ্যা)
            const chars = text.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9\u0980-\u09FF]/g, '');
            document.getElementById('totalChars').textContent = chars.length;
            
            // Vowel গণনা
            const vowels = text.match(/[aeiouAEIOU]/g) || [];
            document.getElementById('totalVowels').textContent = vowels.length;
            
            // Consonant গণনা (মোট অক্ষর - vowel)
            const consonants = chars.length - vowels.length;
            document.getElementById('totalConsonants').textContent = consonants;
            
            // পৃথক vowel গণনা
            const countA = (text.match(/[aA]/g) || []).length;
            const countE = (text.match(/[eE]/g) || []).length;
            const countI = (text.match(/[iI]/g) || []).length;
            const countO = (text.match(/[oO]/g) || []).length;
            const countU = (text.match(/[uU]/g) || []).length;
            
            document.getElementById('countA').textContent = countA;
            document.getElementById('countE').textContent = countE;
            document.getElementById('countI').textContent = countI;
            document.getElementById('countO').textContent = countO;
            document.getElementById('countU').textContent = countU;
        }

        document.getElementById('textInput').addEventListener('input', countVowels);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🌡️ টেম্পারেচার কনভার্টার</h1>
        
        <div class="converter-box">
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>তাপমাত্রা:</label>
                <input type="number" id="tempInput" placeholder="তাপমাত্রা লিখুন" value="0">
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>যে ইউনিট থেকে:</label>
                <select id="fromUnit">
                    <option value="celsius">সেলসিয়াস (°C)</option>
                    <option value="fahrenheit">ফারেনহাইট (°F)</option>
                    <option value="kelvin">কেলভিন (K)</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>যে ইউনিটে:</label>
                <select id="toUnit">
                    <option value="fahrenheit">ফারেনহাইট (°F)</option>
                    <option value="celsius">সেলসিয়াস (°C)</option>
                    <option value="kelvin">কেলভিন (K)</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <button class="convert-btn" id="convertBtn">কনভার্ট করুন</button>
            
            <div class="result">
                <div class="result-label">ফলাফল:</div>
                <div class="result-value" id="result">32 °F</div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="formula" id="formula">
                °F = (°C × 9/5) + 32
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function convertTemperature() {
            const temp = parseFloat(document.getElementById('tempInput').value);
            const fromUnit = document.getElementById('fromUnit').value;
            const toUnit = document.getElementById('toUnit').value;
            
            let celsius, result, formula;
            
            // প্রথমে সেলসিয়াসে কনভার্ট করি
            if (fromUnit === 'celsius') {
                celsius = temp;
            } else if (fromUnit === 'fahrenheit') {
                celsius = (temp - 32) * 5/9;
            } else if (fromUnit === 'kelvin') {
                celsius = temp - 273.15;
            }
            
            // সেলসিয়াস থেকে কাঙ্ক্ষিত ইউনিটে কনভার্ট
            if (toUnit === 'celsius') {
                result = celsius;
                formula = `${temp}°${fromUnit === 'celsius' ? 'C' : fromUnit === 'fahrenheit' ? 'F' : 'K'} = ${celsius.toFixed(2)}°C`;
            } else if (toUnit === 'fahrenheit') {
                result = celsius * 9/5 + 32;
                formula = `${temp}°${fromUnit === 'celsius' ? 'C' : fromUnit === 'fahrenheit' ? 'F' : 'K'} = ${result.toFixed(2)}°F`;
            } else if (toUnit === 'kelvin') {
                result = celsius + 273.15;
                formula = `${temp}°${fromUnit === 'celsius' ? 'C' : fromUnit === 'fahrenheit' ? 'F' : 'K'} = ${result.toFixed(2)}K`;
            }
            
            document.getElementById('result').textContent = result.toFixed(2) + 
                (toUnit === 'celsius' ? ' °C' : toUnit === 'fahrenheit' ? ' °F' : ' K');
            document.getElementById('formula').textContent = formula;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('convertBtn').addEventListener('click', convertTemperature);
        document.getElementById('tempInput').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') convertTemperature();
        });
        
        convertTemperature(); // প্রাথমিক মান দেখানোর জন্য
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ১০: BMI ক্যালকুলেটর

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>BMI ক্যালকুলেটর</title>
    <style>
        body {

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>⚖️ BMI ক্যালকুলেটর</h1>
        
        <div class="unit-toggle">
            <button class="unit-btn active" id="metricBtn">মেট্রিক</button>
            <button class="unit-btn" id="imperialBtn">ইম্পেরিয়াল</button>
        </div>
        
        <div id="metricInputs">
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>ওজন (কেজি):</label>
                <input type="number" id="weightKg" placeholder="যেমন: 70" value="70">
            </div>
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>উচ্চতা (সেমি):</label>
                <input type="number" id="heightCm" placeholder="যেমন: 170" value="170">
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div id="imperialInputs" style="display: none;">
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>ওজন (পাউন্ড):</label>
                <input type="number" id="weightLb" placeholder="যেমন: 154" value="154">
            </div>
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>উচ্চতা (ফুট):</label>
                <input type="number" id="heightFt" placeholder="ফুট" value="5">
            </div>
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>উচ্চতা (ইঞ্চি):</label>
                <input type="number" id="heightIn" placeholder="ইঞ্চি" value="7">
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <button class="calculate-btn" id="calculateBtn">BMI গণনা করুন</button>
        
        <div class="result" id="result">
            <div class="bmi-value" id="bmiValue">24.2</div>
            <div class="bmi-category" id="bmiCategory">স্বাভাবিক ওজন</div>
            <div class="bmi-range" id="bmiRange">স্বাস্থ্যকর BMI: 18.5 - 24.9</div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let isMetric = true;
        
        function toggleUnit(metric) {
            isMetric = metric;
            document.getElementById('metricBtn').classList.toggle('active', metric);
            document.getElementById('imperialBtn').classList.toggle('active', !metric);
            document.getElementById('metricInputs').style.display = metric ? 'block' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('imperialInputs').style.display = metric ? 'none' : 'block';
            calculateBMI();
        }
        
        function calculateBMI() {
            let bmi;
            let category;
            let resultClass;
            
            if (isMetric) {
                const weight = parseFloat(document.getElementById('weightKg').value);
                const height = parseFloat(document.getElementById('heightCm').value) / 100; // মিটারে
                bmi = weight / (height * height);
            } else {
                const weight = parseFloat(document.getElementById('weightLb').value);
                const heightFt = parseFloat(document.getElementById('heightFt').value);
                const heightIn = parseFloat(document.getElementById('heightIn').value);
                const heightInches = (heightFt * 12) + heightIn;
                bmi = (weight / (heightInches * heightInches)) * 703;
            }
            
            bmi = bmi.toFixed(1);
            
            if (bmi < 18.5) {
                category = 'ওজন কম';
                resultClass = 'underweight';
            } else if (bmi >= 18.5 && bmi < 25) {
                category = 'স্বাভাবিক ওজন';
                resultClass = 'normal';
            } else if (bmi >= 25 && bmi < 30) {
                category = 'ওজন বেশি';
                resultClass = 'overweight';
            } else {
                category = 'স্থূল';
                resultClass = 'obese';
            }
            
            const resultDiv = document.getElementById('result');
            resultDiv.className = `result ${resultClass}`;
            document.getElementById('bmiValue').textContent = bmi;
            document.getElementById('bmiCategory').textContent = category;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('metricBtn').addEventListener('click', () => toggleUnit(true));
        document.getElementById('imperialBtn').addEventListener('click', () => toggleUnit(false));
        document.getElementById('calculateBtn').addEventListener('click', calculateBMI);
        
        // ইনপুট পরিবর্তন হলে স্বয়ংক্রিয়ভাবে গণনা
        document.querySelectorAll('input').forEach(input => {
            input.addEventListener('input', calculateBMI);
        });
        
        calculateBMI();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">

    <script>
        function generatePassword() {
            const length = document.getElementById('length').value;
            const hasUpper = document.getElementById('uppercase').checked;
            const hasLower = document.getElementById('lowercase').checked;
            const hasNumbers = document.getElementById('numbers').checked;
            const hasSymbols = document.getElementById('symbols').checked;
            
            let charset = '';
            let password = '';
            
            if (hasUpper) charset += 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ';
            if (hasLower) charset += 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
            if (hasNumbers) charset += '0123456789';
            if (hasSymbols) charset += '!@#$%^&*()_+-=[]{}|;:,.<>?';
            
            if (charset === '') {
                alert('কমপক্ষে একটি অপশন সিলেক্ট করুন');
                return;
            }
            
            for (let i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                const randomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * charset.length);
                password += charset[randomIndex];
            }
            
            document.getElementById('password').value = password;
            checkStrength(password);
        }
        
        function copyPassword() {
            const password = document.getElementById('password');
            password.select();
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(password.value).then(() => {
                alert('পাসওয়ার্ড কপি হয়েছে!');
            });
        }
        
        function checkStrength(password) {
            let strength = 0;
            const fill = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
            const text = document.getElementById('strengthText');
            
            // দৈর্ঘ্য
            if (password.length >= 8) strength++;
            if (password.length >= 12) strength++;
            
            // বড় হাতের অক্ষর
            if (/[A-Z]/.test(password)) strength++;
            
            // ছোট হাতের অক্ষর
            if (/[a-z]/.test(password)) strength++;
            
            // সংখ্যা
            if (/[0-9]/.test(password)) strength++;
            
            // প্রতীক
            if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(password)) strength++;
            
            // শক্তি নির্ধারণ
            const percentage = (strength / 6) * 100;
            fill.style.width = percentage + '%';
            
            if (percentage < 40) {
                fill.style.background = '#f44336';
                text.textContent = 'দুর্বল';
            } else if (percentage < 70) {
                fill.style.background = '#ff9800';
                text.textContent = 'মাঝারি';
            } else {
                fill.style.background = '#4caf50';
                text.textContent = 'শক্তিশালী';
            }
        }
        
        document.getElementById('generateBtn').addEventListener('click', generatePassword);
        document.getElementById('copyBtn').addEventListener('click', copyPassword);
        
        // প্রাথমিক পাসওয়ার্ডের শক্তি চেক
        checkStrength('P@ssw0rd123');
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ১২: মেমরি গেম
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>মেমরি গেম</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff6b6b 0%, #ff8e8e 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            max-width: 600px;
            width: 90%;
            text-align: center;
        }
        h1 {
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        .stats {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-around;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        .stat {
            text-align: center;
        }
        .stat-value {
            font-size: 24px;
            font-weight: bold;
            color: #ff6b6b;
        }
        .stat-label {
            color: #666;
        }

            display: grid;

            gap: 10px;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        .card {

            display: flex;

            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(255,107,107,0.3);
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🧠 মেমরি গেম</h1>
        
        <div class="stats">
            <div class="stat">
                <div class="stat-value" id="moves">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">চাল</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat">
                <div class="stat-value" id="matched">0</div>
                <div class="stat-label">মিলেছে</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat">
                <div class="stat-value" id="remaining">16</div>
                <div class="stat-label">বাকি</div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="game-board" id="gameBoard"></div>
        
        <button class="new-game-btn" id="newGameBtn">নতুন খেলা</button>
    </div>

    <script>
        const emojis = ['🐶', '🐱', '🐭', '🐹', '🐰', '🦊', '🐻', '🐼'];
        let cards = [];
        let flippedCards = [];
        let matchedPairs = 0;
        let moves = 0;
        let lockBoard = false;
        
        function initGame() {
            // ইমোজিগুলো দ্বিগুণ করি
            cards = [...emojis, ...emojis];
            
            // শাফল করি
            for (let i = cards.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
                const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
                [cards[i], cards[j]] = [cards[j], cards[i]];
            }
            
            flippedCards = [];
            matchedPairs = 0;
            moves = 0;
            lockBoard = false;
            
            updateStats();
            renderBoard();
        }
        
        function renderBoard() {
            const board = document.getElementById('gameBoard');
            board.innerHTML = '';
            
            cards.forEach((emoji, index) => {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'card';
                card.dataset.index = index;
                card.dat0aset.emoji = emoji;
                card.textContent = '?';
                
                card.addEventListener('click', () => flipCard(index));
                board.appendChild(card);
            });
        }
        
        function flipCard(index) {
            if (lockBoard) return;
            
            const card = document.querySelector(`[data-index="${index}"]`);
            
            // ইতিমধ্যে ফ্লিপ করা বা ম্যাচ করা কার্ড
            if (card.classList.contains('flipped') || card.classList.contains('matched')) {
                return;
            }
            
            // একই কার্ড দুইবার ফ্লিপ করা
            if (flippedCards.includes(index)) return;
            
            card.textContent = cards[index];
            card.classList.add('flipped');
            flippedCards.push(index);
            
            if (flippedCards.length === 2) {
                moves++;
                updateStats();
                checkMatch();
            }
        }
        
        function checkMatch() {
            lockBoard = true;
            
            const [index1, index2] = flippedCards;
            const card1 = document.querySelector(`[data-index="${index1}"]`);
            const card2 = document.querySelector(`[data-index="${index2}"]`);
            
            if (cards[index1] === cards[index2]) {
                // ম্যাচ হয়েছে
                setTimeout(() => {
                    card1.classList.add('matched');
                    card2.classList.add('matched');
                    card1.classList.remove('flipped');
                    card2.classList.remove('flipped');
                    
                    matchedPairs++;
                    updateStats();
                    flippedCards = [];
                    lockBoard = false;
                    
                    if (matchedPairs === emojis.length) {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            alert('🎉 অভিনন্দন! আপনি জিতেছেন!');
                        }, 500);
                    }
                }, 500);
            } else {
                // ম্যাচ হয়নি
                setTimeout(() => {
                    card1.textContent = '?';
                    card2.textContent = '?';
                    card1.classList.remove('flipped');
                    card2.classList.remove('flipped');
                    
                    flippedCards = [];
                    lockBoard = false;
                }, 1000);
            }
        }
        
        function updateStats() {
            document.getElementById('moves').textContent = moves;
            document.getElementById('matched').textContent = matchedPairs;
            document.getElementById('remaining').textContent = (emojis.length - matchedPairs) * 2;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('newGameBtn').addEventListener('click', initGame);
        
        initGame();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        body {

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🎮 টিক-ট্যাক-টো</h1>
        
        <div class="scoreboard">
            <div class="score">
                <div class="score-value" id="xScore">0</div>
                <div class="score-label">X জিতেছে</div>
            </div>
            <div class="score">
                <div class="score-value" id="oScore">0</div>
                <div class="score-label">O জিতেছে</div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="game-status" id="status">X এর পালা</div>
        
        <div class="board" id="board">
            <div class="cell" data-index="0"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="1"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="2"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="3"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="4"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="5"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="6"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="7"></div>
            <div class="cell" data-index="8"></div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="controls">
            <button id="newGameBtn">নতুন খেলা</button>
            <button id="resetBtn">রিসেট স্কোর</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let board = ['', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', ''];
        let currentPlayer = 'X';
        let gameActive = true;
        let xScore = 0;
        let oScore = 0;
        
        const winningConditions = [
            [0, 1, 2], [3, 4, 5], [6, 7, 8], // rows
            [0, 3, 6], [1, 4, 7], [2, 5, 8], // columns
            [0, 4, 8], [2, 4, 6] // diagonals
        ];
        
        function handleCellClick(index) {
            if (!gameActive || board[index] !== '') return;
            
            board[index] = currentPlayer;
            const cell = document.querySelector(`[data-index="${index}"]`);
            cell.textContent = currentPlayer;
            cell.classList.add(currentPlayer.toLowerCase());
            
            checkResult();
        }
        
        function checkResult() {
            let roundWon = false;
            let winningCombo = [];
            
            for (let i = 0; i < winningConditions.length; i++) {
                const [a, b, c] = winningConditions[i];
                if (board[a] && board[a] === board[b] && board[a] === board[c]) {
                    roundWon = true;
                    winningCombo = [a, b, c];
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            if (roundWon) {
                document.getElementById('status').textContent = `${currentPlayer} জিতেছে!`;
                gameActive = false;
                
                // বিজয়ী সেল হাইলাইট
                winningCombo.forEach(index => {
                    document.querySelector(`[data-index="${index}"]`).classList.add('win');
                });
                
                // স্কোর আপডেট
                if (currentPlayer === 'X') {
                    xScore++;
                    document.getElementById('xScore').textContent = xScore;
                } else {
                    oScore++;
                    document.getElementById('oScore').textContent = oScore;
                }
                
                return;
            }
            
            if (!board.includes('')) {
                document.getElementById('status').textContent = 'খেলা ড্র!';
                gameActive = false;
                return;
            }
            
            currentPlayer = currentPlayer === 'X' ? 'O' : 'X';
            document.getElementById('status').textContent = `${currentPlayer} এর পালা`;
        }
        
        function newGame() {
            board = ['', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', ''];
            currentPlayer = 'X';
            gameActive = true;
            document.getElementById('status').textContent = 'X এর পালা';
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.cell').forEach(cell => {
                cell.textContent = '';
                cell.classList.remove('x', 'o', 'win');
            });
        }
        
        function resetScore() {
            xScore = 0;
            oScore = 0;
            document.getElementById('xScore').textContent = xScore;
            document.getElementById('oScore').textContent = oScore;
            newGame();
        }
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.cell').forEach(cell => {
            cell.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const index = cell.dataset.index;
                handleCellClick(index);
            });
        });
        
        document.getElementById('newGameBtn').addEventListener('click', newGame);
        document.getElementById('resetBtn').addEventListener('click', resetScore);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>📅 ক্যালেন্ডার</h1>
        
        <div class="calendar-header">
            <button class="nav-btn" id="prevMonth">←</button>
            <span class="month-year" id="monthYear"></span>
            <button class="nav-btn" id="nextMonth">→</button>
        </div>

            <div>রবি</div>

            <div>শনি</div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="calendar-grid" id="calendarGrid"></div>
        
        <div class="event-form">
            <h3>ইভেন্ট যোগ করুন</h3>
            <div class="event-input">
                <input type="date" id="eventDate">
                <input type="text" id="eventText" placeholder="ইভেন্টের বিবরণ">
                <button id="addEventBtn">যোগ করুন</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let currentDate = new Date();
        let events = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('events')) || {};
        
        function renderCalendar() {
            const year = currentDate.getFullYear();
            const month = currentDate.getMonth();
            
            // মাস ও বছর দেখান
            const months = ['জানুয়ারি', 'ফেব্রুয়ারি', 'মার্চ', 'এপ্রিল', 'মে', 'জুন', 'জুলাই', 'আগস্ট', 'সেপ্টেম্বর', 'অক্টোবর', 'নভেম্বর', 'ডিসেম্বর'];
            document.getElementById('monthYear').textContent = `${months[month]} ${year}`;
            
            // মাসের প্রথম দিন
            const firstDay = new Date(year, month, 1);
            const lastDay = new Date(year, month + 1, 0);
            
            // আগের মাসের শেষ কয়েক দিন
            const prevMonthLastDay = new Date(year, month, 0);
            
            const firstDayIndex = firstDay.getDay(); // 0 = রবিবার
            const lastDayIndex = lastDay.getDay();
            
            const calendarGrid = document.getElementById('calendarGrid');
            calendarGrid.innerHTML = '';
            
            // আগের মাসের দিন
            for (let i = firstDayIndex; i > 0; i--) {
                const day = prevMonthLastDay.getDate() - i + 1;
                const cell = createDayCell(day, true, year, month - 1);
                calendarGrid.appendChild(cell);
            }
            
            // বর্তমান মাসের দিন
            for (let i = 1; i <= lastDay.getDate(); i++) {
                const cell = createDayCell(i, false, year, month);
                calendarGrid.appendChild(cell);
            }
            
            // পরের মাসের দিন
            const nextMonthDays = 42 - (firstDayIndex + lastDay.getDate());
            for (let i = 1; i <= nextMonthDays; i++) {
                const cell = createDayCell(i, true, year, month + 1);
                calendarGrid.appendChild(cell);
            }
        }
        
        function createDayCell(day, isOtherMonth, year, month) {
            const cell = document.createElement('div');
            cell.className = `calendar-day ${isOtherMonth ? 'other-month' : ''}`;
            
            const dateStr = `${year}-${String(month + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(day).padStart(2, '0')}`;
            
            // আজকের তারিখ চেক
            const today = new Date();
            if (!isOtherMonth && 
                day === today.getDate() && 
                month === today.getMonth() && 
                year === today.getFullYear()) {
                cell.classList.add('today');
            }
            
            cell.innerHTML = `<span class="day-number">${day}</span>`;
            
            // ইভেন্ট আছে কিনা চেক
            if (events[dateStr]) {
                const indicator = document.createElement('div');
                indicator.className = 'event-indicator';
                cell.appendChild(indicator);
                
                // টুলটিপ
                cell.title = events[dateStr];
            }
            
            cell.addEventListener('click', () => {
                document.getElementById('eventDate').value = dateStr;
            });
            
            return cell;
        }
        
        function changeMonth(direction) {
            currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() + direction);
            renderCalendar();
        }
        
        function addEvent() {
            const date = document.getElementById('eventDate').value;
            const eventText = document.getElementById('eventText').value;
            
            if (date && eventText) {
                events[date] = eventText;
                localStorage.setItem('events', JSON.stringify(events));
                renderCalendar();
                document.getElementById('eventText').value = '';
            } else {
                alert('তারিখ এবং ইভেন্টের বিবরণ দিন');
            }
        }
        
        document.getElementById('prevMonth').addEventListener('click', () => changeMonth(-1));
        document.getElementById('nextMonth').addEventListener('click', () => changeMonth(1));
        document.getElementById('addEventBtn').addEventListener('click', addEvent);
        
        renderCalendar();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>স্টপওয়াচ</title>
    <style>
        body {

        }

            color: #666;
        }
        .lap-time {
            font-weight: bold;
            color: #43e97b;
            font-family: monospace;
        }
    </style>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>⏱️ স্টপওয়াচ</h1>
        
        <div class="stopwatch">
            <div class="time-display" id="display">00:00:00.00</div>
            
            <div class="controls">
                <button id="startBtn">শুরু</button>
                <button id="pauseBtn" disabled>বিরতি</button>
                <button id="resetBtn">রিসেট</button>
                <button id="lapBtn">ল্যাপ</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="laps" id="laps"></div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let startTime;
        let updatedTime;
        let difference;
        let timerInterval;
        let running = false;
        let paused = false;
        let lapCounter = 1;
        
        const display = document.getElementById('display');
        const startBtn = document.getElementById('startBtn');
        const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('pauseBtn');
        const resetBtn = document.getElementById('resetBtn');
        const lapBtn = document.getElementById('lapBtn');
        const lapsContainer = document.getElementById('laps');
        
        function startTimer() {
            if (!running) {
                startTime = new Date().getTime();
                timerInterval = setInterval(updateTimer, 10);
                running = true;
                paused = false;
                
                startBtn.disabled = true;
                pauseBtn.disabled = false;
                pauseBtn.textContent = 'বিরতি';
            }
        }
        
        function pauseTimer() {
            if (running && !paused) {
                clearInterval(timerInterval);
                paused = true;
                pauseBtn.textContent = 'চালু';
            } else if (running && paused) {
                startTime = new Date().getTime() - (updatedTime - startTime);
                timerInterval = setInterval(updateTimer, 10);
                paused = false;
                pauseBtn.textContent = 'বিরতি';
            }
        }
        
        function resetTimer() {
            clearInterval(timerInterval);
            running = false;
            paused = false;
            display.textContent = '00:00:00.00';
            startBtn.disabled = false;
            pauseBtn.disabled = true;
            pauseBtn.textContent = 'বিরতি';
            lapCounter = 1;
            lapsContainer.innerHTML = '';
        }
        
        function updateTimer() {
            updatedTime = new Date().getTime();
            difference = updatedTime - startTime;
            
            let hours = Math.floor(difference / (1000 * 60 * 60));
            let minutes = Math.floor((difference % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
            let seconds = Math.floor((difference % (1000 * 60)) / 1000);
            let milliseconds = Math.floor((difference % 1000) / 10);
            
            hours = hours.toString().padStart(2, '0');
            minutes = minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0');
            seconds = seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0');
            milliseconds = milliseconds.toString().padStart(2, '0');
            
            display.textContent = `${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}.${milliseconds}`;
        }
        
        function addLap() {
            if (running) {
                const lapTime = display.textContent;
                const lapItem = document.createElement('div');
                lapItem.className = 'lap-item';
                lapItem.innerHTML = `
                    <span class="lap-number">ল্যাপ ${lapCounter}</span>
                    <span class="lap-time">${lapTime}</span>
                `;
                lapsContainer.insertBefore(lapItem, lapsContainer.firstChild);
                lapCounter++;
            }
        }
        
        startBtn.addEventListener('click', startTimer);
        pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', pauseTimer);
        resetBtn.addEventListener('click', resetTimer);
        lapBtn.addEventListener('click', addLap);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>💰 মুদ্রা কনভার্টার</h1>
        
        <div class="converter-box">
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>পরিমাণ:</label>
                <input type="number" id="amount" value="1" min="0" step="0.01">
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>যে মুদ্রা থেকে:</label>
                <select id="fromCurrency">
                    <option value="USD">USD - মার্কিন ডলার</option>
                    <option value="EUR">EUR - ইউরো</option>
                    <option value="GBP">GBP - ব্রিটিশ পাউন্ড</option>
                    <option value="JPY">JPY - জাপানি ইয়েন</option>
                    <option value="BDT" selected>BDT - বাংলাদেশি টাকা</option>
                    <option value="INR">INR - ভারতীয় রুপি</option>
                    <option value="CAD">CAD - কানাডিয়ান ডলার</option>
                    <option value="AUD">AUD - অস্ট্রেলিয়ান ডলার</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <div class="swap-btn">
                <button id="swapBtn">⇅</button>
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>যে মুদ্রায়:</label>
                <select id="toCurrency">
                    <option value="USD" selected>USD - মার্কিন ডলার</option>
                    <option value="EUR">EUR - ইউরো</option>
                    <option value="GBP">GBP - ব্রিটিশ পাউন্ড</option>
                    <option value="JPY">JPY - জাপানি ইয়েন</option>
                    <option value="BDT">BDT - বাংলাদেশি টাকা</option>
                    <option value="INR">INR - ভারতীয় রুপি</option>
                    <option value="CAD">CAD - কানাডিয়ান ডলার</option>
                    <option value="AUD">AUD - অস্ট্রেলিয়ান ডলার</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <button class="convert-btn" id="convertBtn">কনভার্ট করুন</button>
            
            <div class="result">
                <div class="result-label" id="resultLabel">1 BDT =</div>
                <div class="result-value" id="result">0.0091 USD</div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="last-updated" id="lastUpdated"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // ডামি এক্সচেঞ্জ রেট (API না থাকলে ব্যবহারের জন্য)
        const exchangeRates = {
            USD: 1,
            EUR: 0.92,
            GBP: 0.79,
            JPY: 150.5,
            BDT: 110.0,
            INR: 83.0,
            CAD: 1.35,
            AUD: 1.52
        };
        
        let lastUpdated = new Date().toLocaleString();
        
        function convertCurrency() {
            const amount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('amount').value);
            const fromCurrency = document.getElementById('fromCurrency').value;
            const toCurrency = document.getElementById('toCurrency').value;
            
            // প্রথমে USD এ কনভার্ট, তারপর টার্গেট কারেন্সিতে
            const amountInUSD = amount / exchangeRates[fromCurrency];
            const result = amountInUSD * exchangeRates[toCurrency];
            
            document.getElementById('resultLabel').textContent = 
                `${amount} ${fromCurrency} =`;
            document.getElementById('result').textContent = 
                `${result.toFixed(2)} ${toCurrency}`;
        }
        
        function swapCurrencies() {
            const fromSelect = document.getElementById('fromCurrency');
            const toSelect = document.getElementById('toCurrency');
            
            const fromValue = fromSelect.value;
            fromSelect.value = toSelect.value;
            toSelect.value = fromValue;
            
            convertCurrency();
        }
        
        function updateLastUpdated() {
            document.getElementById('lastUpdated').textContent = 
                `সর্বশেষ আপডেট: ${lastUpdated}`;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('convertBtn').addEventListener('click', convertCurrency);
        document.getElementById('swapBtn').addEventListener('click', swapCurrencies);
        document.getElementById('amount').addEventListener('input', convertCurrency);
        
        convertCurrency();
        updateLastUpdated();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <style>
        body {

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>📏 ইউনিট কনভার্টার</h1>
        
        <div class="converter-box">
            <div class="category-select">
                <select id="category">
                    <option value="length">দৈর্ঘ্য</option>
                    <option value="weight">ওজন</option>
                    <option value="volume">আয়তন</option>
                    <option value="area">ক্ষেত্রফল</option>
                    <option value="speed">গতিবেগ</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>পরিমাণ:</label>
                <input type="number" id="amount" value="1" min="0" step="any">
            </div>
            
            <div class="unit-row">
                <select id="fromUnit"></select>
                <select id="toUnit"></select>
            </div>
            
            <button class="convert-btn" id="convertBtn">কনভার্ট করুন</button>
            
            <div class="result">
                <div class="result-value" id="result">1</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const units = {
            length: {
                meter: 1,
                kilometer: 1000,
                centimeter: 0.01,
                millimeter: 0.001,
                mile: 1609.34,
                yard: 0.9144,
                foot: 0.3048,
                inch: 0.0254
            },
            weight: {
                kilogram: 1,
                gram: 0.001,
                milligram: 0.000001,
                pound: 0.453592,
                ounce: 0.0283495
            },
            volume: {
                liter: 1,
                milliliter: 0.001,
                gallon: 3.78541,
                quart: 0.946353,
                pint: 0.473176,
                cup: 0.236588
            },
            area: {
                squareMeter: 1,
                squareKilometer: 1000000,
                squareFoot: 0.092903,
                squareInch: 0.00064516,
                acre: 4046.86,
                hectare: 10000
            },
            speed: {
                meterPerSecond: 1,
                kilometerPerHour: 0.277778,
                milePerHour: 0.44704,
                knot: 0.514444
            }
        };
        
        const unitNames = {
            length: {
                meter: 'মিটার',
                kilometer: 'কিলোমিটার',
                centimeter: 'সেন্টিমিটার',
                millimeter: 'মিলিমিটার',
                mile: 'মাইল',
                yard: 'গজ',
                foot: 'ফুট',
                inch: 'ইঞ্চি'
            },
            weight: {
                kilogram: 'কিলোগ্রাম',
                gram: 'গ্রাম',
                milligram: 'মিলিগ্রাম',
                pound: 'পাউন্ড',
                ounce: 'আউন্স'
            },
            volume: {
                liter: 'লিটার',
                milliliter: 'মিলিলিটার',
                gallon: 'গ্যালন',
                quart: 'কোয়ার্ট',
                pint: 'পিন্ট',
                cup: 'কাপ'
            },
            area: {
                squareMeter: 'বর্গমিটার',
                squareKilometer: 'বর্গকিলোমিটার',
                squareFoot: 'বর্গফুট',
                squareInch: 'বর্গইঞ্চি',
                acre: 'একর',
                hectare: 'হেক্টর'
            },
            speed: {
                meterPerSecond: 'মিটার/সেকেন্ড',
                kilometerPerHour: 'কিলোমিটার/ঘণ্টা',
                milePerHour: 'মাইল/ঘণ্টা',
                knot: 'নট'
            }
        };
        
        function updateUnitSelectors() {
            const category = document.getElementById('category').value;
            const fromSelect = document.getElementById('fromUnit');
            const toSelect = document.getElementById('toUnit');
            
            fromSelect.innerHTML = '';
            toSelect.innerHTML = '';
            
            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(units[category])) {
                const option1 = document.createElement('option');
                option1.value = key;
                option1.textContent = unitNames[category][key];
                fromSelect.appendChild(option1);
                
                const option2 = document.createElement('option');
                option2.value = key;
                option2.textContent = unitNames[category][key];
                toSelect.appendChild(option2);
            }
            
            // ডিফল্ট নির্বাচন
            if (category === 'length') {
                fromSelect.value = 'meter';
                toSelect.value = 'kilometer';
            } else if (category === 'weight') {
                fromSelect.value = 'kilogram';
                toSelect.value = 'gram';
            } else if (category === 'volume') {
                fromSelect.value = 'liter';
                toSelect.value = 'milliliter';
            } else if (category === 'area') {
                fromSelect.value = 'squareMeter';
                toSelect.value = 'squareKilometer';
            } else if (category === 'speed') {
                fromSelect.value = 'meterPerSecond';
                toSelect.value = 'kilometerPerHour';
            }
            
            convert();
        }
        
        function convert() {
            const category = document.getElementById('category').value;
            const amount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('amount').value) || 0;
            const fromUnit = document.getElementById('fromUnit').value;
            const toUnit = document.getElementById('toUnit').value;
            
            // প্রথমে বেস ইউনিটে (যেমন মিটার, কেজি) কনভার্ট
            const baseValue = amount * units[category][fromUnit];
            
            // বেস ইউনিট থেকে টার্গেট ইউনিটে কনভার্ট
            const result = baseValue / units[category][toUnit];
            
            document.getElementById('result').textContent = 
                `${result.toFixed(4)} ${unitNames[category][toUnit]}`;
        }
        
        document.getElementById('category').addEventListener('change', updateUnitSelectors);
        document.getElementById('amount').addEventListener('input', convert);
        document.getElementById('fromUnit').addEventListener('change', convert);
        document.getElementById('toUnit').addEventListener('change', convert);
        document.getElementById('convertBtn').addEventListener('click', convert);
        
        updateUnitSelectors();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <div class="container">
        <h1>🎂 এজ ক্যালকুলেটর</h1>
        
        <div class="calculator-box">

                <input type="date" id="birthDate">
            </div>
            
            <button class="calculate-btn" id="calculateBtn">বয়স গণনা করুন</button>
            
            <div class="result-grid">
                <div class="result-card years">
                    <div class="result-value" id="years">0</div>
                    <div class="result-label">বছর</div>
                </div>

                    <div class="result-value" id="months">0</div>

                </div>

                <div class="info-row">

                    <span class="info-value" id="totalHours">0</span>
                </div>
                <div class="info-row">
                    <span class="info-label">মোট মিনিট:</span>
                    <span class="info-value" id="totalMinutes">0</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="next-birthday" id="nextBirthday"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function calculateAge() {
            const birthDate = new Date(document.getElementById('birthDate').value);
            const today = new Date();
            
            if (isNaN(birthDate.getTime())) {
                alert('দয়া করে জন্ম তারিখ নির্বাচন করুন');
                return;
            }
            
            // বয়স গণনা (বছর, মাস, দিন)
            let years = today.getFullYear() - birthDate.getFullYear();
            let months = today.getMonth() - birthDate.getMonth();
            let days = today.getDate() - birthDate.getDate();
            
            if (months < 0 || (months === 0 && days < 0)) {
                years--;
                months += 12;
            }
            
            if (days < 0) {
                const lastMonth = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - 1, 0);
                days += lastMonth.getDate();
                months--;
            }
            
            document.getElementById('years').textContent = years;
            document.getElementById('months').textContent = months;
            document.getElementById('days').textContent = days;
            
            // মোট দিন
            const diffTime = Math.abs(today - birthDate);
            const totalDays = Math.floor(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
            document.getElementById('totalDays').textContent = totalDays.toLocaleString();
            
            // মোট মাস
            const totalMonths = years * 12 + months;
            document.getElementById('totalMonths').textContent = totalMonths;
            
            // মোট সপ্তাহ
            const totalWeeks = Math.floor(totalDays / 7);
            document.getElementById('totalWeeks').textContent = totalWeeks;
            
            // মোট ঘণ্টা
            const totalHours = totalDays * 24;
            document.getElementById('totalHours').textContent = totalHours.toLocaleString();
            
            // মোট মিনিট
            const totalMinutes = totalHours * 60;
            document.getElementById('totalMinutes').textContent = totalMinutes.toLocaleString();
            
            // পরবর্তী জন্মদিন
            const nextBirthday = new Date(today.getFullYear(), birthDate.getMonth(), birthDate.getDate());
            if (nextBirthday < today) {
                nextBirthday.setFullYear(nextBirthday.getFullYear() + 1);
            }
            
            const daysUntilBirthday = Math.ceil((nextBirthday - today) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
            const monthsUntilBirthday = Math.floor(daysUntilBirthday / 30);
            const daysRemaining = daysUntilBirthday % 30;
            
            const birthdayElement = document.getElementById('nextBirthday');
            birthdayElement.innerHTML = `
                <strong>পরবর্তী জন্মদিন:</strong> ${nextBirthday.toLocaleDateString('bn-BD')}<br>
                <strong>বাকি আছে:</strong> ${monthsUntilBirthday} মাস ${daysRemaining} দিন
            `;
        }
        
        // আজকের তারিখ ডিফল্ট হিসেবে সেট করুন
        const today = new Date();
        const thirtyYearsAgo = new Date(today.getFullYear() - 30, today.getMonth(), today.getDate());
        const formattedDate = thirtyYearsAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0];
        document.getElementById('birthDate').value = formattedDate;
        
        document.getElementById('calculateBtn').addEventListener('click', calculateAge);
        calculateAge();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>💵 টিপ ক্যালকুলেটর</h1>
        
        <div class="calculator-box">
            <div class="input-group">
                <label>বিলের পরিমাণ:</label>
                <input type="number" id="billAmount" value="1000" min="0" step="any">
            </div>
            
            <div class="tip-buttons">
                <button class="tip-btn" data-tip="10">১০%</button>
                <button class="tip-btn" data-tip="15">১৫%</button>
                <button class="tip-btn" data-tip="20">২০%</button>
                <button class="tip-btn" data-tip="25">২৫%</button>
                <button class="tip-btn active" data-tip="15">১৫%</button>
                <button class="tip-btn" data-tip="custom">কাস্টম</button>
            </div>
            
            <div class="input-group" id="customTipInput" style="display: none;">
                <label>কাস্টম টিপ (%):</label>
                <input type="number" id="customTip" value="15" min="0" step="any">
            </div>
            
            <div class="split-control">
                <button class="split-btn" id="decreaseSplit">-</button>
                <span>
                    <span id="splitCount">1</span> জন
                </span>
                <button class="split-btn" id="increaseSplit">+</button>
            </div>
            
            <div class="result">
                <div class="result-row">
                    <span class="result-label">টিপ (১৫%):</span>
                    <span class="result-value" id="tipAmount">১৫০ টাকা</span>
                </div>
                <div class="result-row">
                    <span class="result-label">মোট বিল:</span>
                    <span class="result-value" id="totalAmount">১১৫০ টাকা</span>
                </div>
                <div class="result-row total">
                    <span class="result-label">প্রতি জনে:</span>
                    <span class="result-value" id="perPerson">১১৫০ টাকা</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let tipPercentage = 15;
        let splitCount = 1;
        
        function calculate() {
            const bill = parseFloat(document.getElementById('billAmount').value) || 0;
            
            // টিপের পরিমাণ
            const tip = (bill * tipPercentage) / 100;
            const total = bill + tip;
            const perPerson = total / splitCount;
            
            // বাংলা সংখ্যায় দেখান
            document.getElementById('tipAmount').textContent = 
                `${tip.toFixed(0)} টাকা`;
            document.getElementById('totalAmount').textContent = 
                `${total.toFixed(0)} টাকা`;
            document.getElementById('perPerson').textContent = 
                `${perPerson.toFixed(0)} টাকা`;
        }
        
        function setTipPercentage(percentage) {
            tipPercentage = percentage;
            
            // বাটন হাইলাইট
            document.querySelectorAll('.tip-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            if (percentage === 'custom') {
                document.getElementById('customTipInput').style.display = 'block';
                tipPercentage = parseFloat(document.getElementById('customTip').value) || 0;
            } else {
                document.getElementById('customTipInput').style.display = 'none';
                event.target.classList.add('active');
            }
            
            calculate();
        }
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.tip-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const tip = e.target.dataset.tip;
                setTipPercentage(tip);
            });
        });
        
        document.getElementById('customTip').addEventListener('input', () => {
            tipPercentage = parseFloat(document.getElementById('customTip').value) || 0;
            calculate();
        });
        
        document.getElementById('billAmount').addEventListener('input', calculate);
        
        document.getElementById('increaseSplit').addEventListener('click', () => {
            splitCount++;
            document.getElementById('splitCount').textContent = splitCount;
            calculate();
        });
        
        document.getElementById('decreaseSplit').addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (splitCount > 1) {
                splitCount--;
                document.getElementById('splitCount').textContent = splitCount;
                calculate();
            }
        });
        
        calculate();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
