            cursor: pointer;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        
        .option:hover {
            background: #f0f0f0;
            border-color: #667eea;
        }
        
        .option.selected {
            background: #667eea;
            color: white;
            border-color: #667eea;
        }
        
        .option.correct {
            background: #43e97b;
            color: white;
            border-color: #43e97b;
        }
        
        .option.wrong {
            background: #f44336;
            color: white;
            border-color: #f44336;
        }
        
        .feedback {
            margin-top: 20px;
            padding: 15px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            display: none;
        }
        
        .feedback.correct {
            background: #d4edda;
            color: #155724;
            display: block;
        }
        
        .feedback.wrong {
            background: #f8d7da;
            color: #721c24;
            display: block;
        }
        
        .controls {
            display: flex;
            gap: 15px;
            justify-content: center;
            margin-top: 30px;
        }
        
        .btn {
            padding: 15px 30px;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 8px;
            cursor: pointer;
            font-size: 16px;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        
        .btn-primary {
            background: #667eea;
            color: white;
        }
        
        .btn-success {
            background: #43e97b;
            color: white;
        }
        
        .btn:hover {
            transform: translateY(-2px);
            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
        }
        
        .btn:disabled {
            opacity: 0.5;
            cursor: not-allowed;
        }
        
        .result-container {
            text-align: center;
            display: none;
        }
        
        .final-score {
            font-size: 48px;
            font-weight: bold;
            color: #667eea;
            margin: 20px 0;
        }
        
        .progress-bar {
            width: 100%;
            height: 10px;
            background: #f0f0f0;
            border-radius: 5px;
            margin-top: 20px;
            overflow: hidden;
        }
        
        .progress-fill {
            height: 100%;
            background: linear-gradient(90deg, #667eea, #764ba2);
            transition: width 0.3s;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>📝 কুইজ অ্যাপ</h1>
        
        <div id="quizContainer">
            <div class="quiz-header">
                <div class="question-number" id="questionNumber">প্রশ্ন ১/১০</div>
                <div class="score" id="score">স্কোর: ০</div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="question-container">
                <div class="question-text" id="question"></div>
                <div class="options" id="options"></div>
                <div class="feedback" id="feedback"></div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="controls">
                <button class="btn btn-primary" id="nextBtn" onclick="nextQuestion()">পরবর্তী</button>
                <button class="btn btn-success" id="restartBtn" onclick="restartQuiz()" style="display: none;">পুনরায় শুরু</button>
            </div>
            
            <div class="progress-bar">
                <div class="progress-fill" id="progressFill"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="result-container" id="resultContainer">
            <h2>কুইজ শেষ!</h2>
            <div class="final-score" id="finalScore">০/১০</div>
            <p id="resultMessage"></p>
            <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="restartQuiz()">আবার খেলুন</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const quizData = [
            {
                question: "জাভাস্ক্রিপ্ট কী?",
                options: ["প্রোগ্রামিং ভাষা", "মার্কআপ ভাষা", "স্টাইল শীট ভাষা", "ডাটাবেস ভাষা"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "HTML এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?",
                options: ["Hyper Text Markup Language", "High Tech Modern Language", "Hyper Transfer Markup Language", "Home Tool Markup Language"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "CSS এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?",
                options: ["Cascading Style Sheets", "Computer Style Sheets", "Creative Style System", "Colorful Style Sheets"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "নিচের কোনটি জাভাস্ক্রিপ্ট ফ্রেমওয়ার্ক?",
                options: ["React", "Django", "Laravel", "Flask"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "DOM এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?",
                options: ["Document Object Model", "Data Object Model", "Document Oriented Model", "Digital Object Management"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "নিচের কোনটি ডাটাবেস?",
                options: ["MongoDB", "Express.js", "React", "Node.js"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "API এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?",
                options: ["Application Programming Interface", "Application Program Interface", "Advanced Programming Interface", "Application Protocol Interface"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "HTTP কী?",
                options: ["Hyper Text Transfer Protocol", "High Text Transfer Protocol", "Hyper Transfer Text Protocol", "Home Text Transfer Protocol"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "JSON এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?",
                options: ["JavaScript Object Notation", "Java Standard Object Notation", "JavaScript Online Notation", "Java Source Object Notation"],
                correct: 0
            },
            {
                question: "নিচের কোনটি ভার্সন কন্ট্রোল সিস্টেম?",
                options: ["Git", "npm", "yarn", "webpack"],
                correct: 0
            }
        ];
        
        let currentQuestion = 0;
        let score = 0;
        let selectedOption = null;
        let quizCompleted = false;
        
        function loadQuestion() {
            if (quizCompleted) return;
            
            const question = quizData[currentQuestion];
            document.getElementById('question').textContent = question.question;
            document.getElementById('questionNumber').textContent = `প্রশ্ন ${currentQuestion + 1}/${quizData.length}`;
            
            const optionsContainer = document.getElementById('options');
            optionsContainer.innerHTML = '';
            
            question.options.forEach((option, index) => {
                const optionDiv = document.createElement('div');
                optionDiv.className = 'option';
                optionDiv.textContent = option;
                optionDiv.onclick = () => selectOption(index);
                optionsContainer.appendChild(optionDiv);
            });
            
            document.getElementById('feedback').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('nextBtn').disabled = true;
            
            updateProgress();
        }
        
        function selectOption(index) {
            if (selectedOption !== null) return;
            
            selectedOption = index;
            const options = document.querySelectorAll('.option');
            options[index].classList.add('selected');
            document.getElementById('nextBtn').disabled = false;
        }
        
        function nextQuestion() {
            if (selectedOption === null) return;
            
            const question = quizData[currentQuestion];
            const options = document.querySelectorAll('.option');
            const feedback = document.getElementById('feedback');
            
            if (selectedOption === question.correct) {
                score++;
                options[selectedOption].classList.add('correct');
                feedback.className = 'feedback correct';
                feedback.textContent = '✅ সঠিক উত্তর!';
            } else {
                options[selectedOption].classList.add('wrong');
                options[question.correct].classList.add('correct');
                feedback.className = 'feedback wrong';
                feedback.textContent = `❌ ভুল! সঠিক উত্তর: ${question.options[question.correct]}`;
            }
            
            feedback.style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('score').textContent = `স্কোর: ${score}`;
            document.getElementById('nextBtn').disabled = true;
            
            selectedOption = null;
            
            if (currentQuestion < quizData.length - 1) {
                currentQuestion++;
                setTimeout(loadQuestion, 2000);
            } else {
                quizCompleted = true;
                setTimeout(showResult, 2000);
            }
        }
        
        function showResult() {
            document.getElementById('quizContainer').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('resultContainer').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('finalScore').textContent = `${score}/${quizData.length}`;
            
            let message;
            const percentage = (score / quizData.length) * 100;
            if (percentage >= 80) {
                message = '🎉 অসাধারণ! আপনি খুব ভালো করেছেন!';
            } else if (percentage >= 60) {
                message = '👍 ভালো করেছেন, আরও অনুশীলন করুন!';
            } else if (percentage >= 40) {
                message = '👌 ঠিক আছে, আরও মনোযোগ দিন!';
            } else {
                message = '💪 চেষ্টা চালিয়ে যান, আপনি পারবেন!';
            }
            document.getElementById('resultMessage').textContent = message;
        }
        
        function restartQuiz() {
            currentQuestion = 0;
            score = 0;
            selectedOption = null;
            quizCompleted = false;
            
            document.getElementById('quizContainer').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('resultContainer').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('score').textContent = 'স্কোর: 0';
            
            loadQuestion();
        }
        
        function updateProgress() {
            const progress = ((currentQuestion) / quizData.length) * 100;
            document.getElementById('progressFill').style.width = progress + '%';
        }
        
        loadQuestion();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <style>

        }
        
        .rating-btn.medium {

        }

            background: #f44336;

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🗂️ ফ্ল্যাশকার্ড</h1>
        
        <div class="category-selector">
            <button class="category-btn active" onclick="changeCategory('all')">সব</button>
            <button class="category-btn" onclick="changeCategory('javascript')">জাভাস্ক্রিপ্ট</button>
            <button class="category-btn" onclick="changeCategory('html')">এইচটিএমএল</button>
            <button class="category-btn" onclick="changeCategory('css')">সিএসএস</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="flashcard-container" onclick="flipCard()">
            <div class="flashcard" id="flashcard">
                <div class="card-face card-front">
                    <div class="card-title" id="frontTitle"></div>
                    <div class="card-content" id="frontContent"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="card-face card-back">
                    <div class="card-title">উত্তর</div>
                    <div class="card-content" id="backContent"></div>
                    <div class="card-example" id="example"></div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="progress">
            <div class="card-counter" id="cardCounter"></div>
            <div class="card-counter">জানা: <span id="knownCount">0</span></div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="controls">
            <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="previousCard()">← পূর্ববর্তী</button>
            <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="nextCard()">পরবর্তী →</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="rating">
            <button class="rating-btn easy" onclick="rateCard('easy')">সহজ</button>
            <button class="rating-btn medium" onclick="rateCard('medium')">মাঝারি</button>
            <button class="rating-btn hard" onclick="rateCard('hard')">কঠিন</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="add-card-form">
            <h3>নতুন ফ্ল্যাশকার্ড যোগ করুন</h3>
            <div class="form-group">
                <label>ক্যাটাগরি:</label>
                <select id="newCategory">
                    <option value="javascript">জাভাস্ক্রিপ্ট</option>
                    <option value="html">এইচটিএমএল</option>
                    <option value="css">সিএসএস</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <label>প্রশ্ন:</label>
                <input type="text" id="newQuestion" placeholder="প্রশ্ন লিখুন">
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <label>উত্তর:</label>
                <textarea id="newAnswer" placeholder="উত্তর লিখুন"></textarea>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
                <label>উদাহরণ:</label>
                <textarea id="newExample" placeholder="উদাহরণ (ঐচ্ছিক)"></textarea>
            </div>
            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="addCard()" style="width: 100%;">কার্ড যোগ করুন</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let flashcards = [
            {
                id: 1,
                category: 'javascript',
                question: 'জাভাস্ক্রিপ্ট কী?',
                answer: 'একটি প্রোগ্রামিং ভাষা যা ওয়েব পেজকে ইন্টারেক্টিভ করে তোলে।',
                example: 'console.log("Hello World");',
                difficulty: 'medium',
                known: false
            },
            {
                id: 2,
                category: 'html',
                question: 'HTML এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?',
                answer: 'Hyper Text Markup Language',
                example: '<p>This is a paragraph</p>',
                difficulty: 'easy',
                known: false
            },
            {
                id: 3,
                category: 'css',
                question: 'CSS এর পূর্ণরূপ কী?',
                answer: 'Cascading Style Sheets',
                example: 'body { color: red; }',
                difficulty: 'easy',
                known: false
            },
            {
                id: 4,
                category: 'javascript',
                question: 'let এবং const এর মধ্যে পার্থক্য কী?',
                answer: 'let দিয়ে ভেরিয়েবলের মান পরিবর্তন করা যায়, const দিয়ে যায় না।',
                example: 'let x = 5; x = 10; (চলে)\nconst y = 5; y = 10; (চলে না)',
                difficulty: 'medium',
                known: false
            }
        ];
        
        let currentCategory = 'all';
        let currentIndex = 0;
        let filteredCards = flashcards;
        
        function filterCards() {
            if (currentCategory === 'all') {
                filteredCards = flashcards;
            } else {
                filteredCards = flashcards.filter(card => card.category === currentCategory);
            }
            
            if (filteredCards.length === 0) {
                filteredCards = [{
                    question: 'কোন কার্ড নেই',
                    answer: 'এই ক্যাটাগরিতে কোনো কার্ড নেই',
                    example: 'নতুন কার্ড যোগ করুন'
                }];
            }
            
            currentIndex = 0;
            updateCard();
            updateCounter();
        }
        
        function changeCategory(category) {
            currentCategory = category;
            document.querySelectorAll('.category-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            filterCards();
        }
        
        function flipCard() {
            document.getElementById('flashcard').classList.toggle('flipped');
        }
        
        function updateCard() {
            const card = filteredCards[currentIndex];
            document.getElementById('frontTitle').textContent = card.category || 'প্রশ্ন';
            document.getElementById('frontContent').textContent = card.question;
            document.getElementById('backContent').textContent = card.answer;
            document.getElementById('example').textContent = card.example || '';
            
            // ফ্লিপ অবস্থা রিসেট
            document.getElementById('flashcard').classList.remove('flipped');
        }
        
        function updateCounter() {
            document.getElementById('cardCounter').textContent = 
                `কার্ড ${currentIndex + 1}/${filteredCards.length}`;
            
            const known = flashcards.filter(c => c.known).length;
            document.getElementById('knownCount').textContent = known;
        }
        
        function nextCard() {
            if (currentIndex < filteredCards.length - 1) {
                currentIndex++;
                updateCard();
                updateCounter();
            }
        }
        
        function previousCard() {
            if (currentIndex > 0) {
                currentIndex--;
                updateCard();
                updateCounter();
            }
        }
        
        function rateCard(difficulty) {
            const card = filteredCards[currentIndex];
            if (card.id) {
                const originalCard = flashcards.find(c => c.id === card.id);
                originalCard.difficulty = difficulty;
                
                if (difficulty === 'easy') {
                    originalCard.known = true;
                }
                
                updateCounter();
            }
        }
        
        function addCard() {
            const category = document.getElementById('newCategory').value;
            const question = document.getElementById('newQuestion').value;
            const answer = document.getElementById('newAnswer').value;
            const example = document.getElementById('newExample').value;
            
            if (question && answer) {
                const newCard = {
                    id: flashcards.length + 1,
                    category: category,
                    question: question,
                    answer: answer,
                    example: example,
                    difficulty: 'medium',
                    known: false
                };
                
                flashcards.push(newCard);
                filterCards();
                
                // ফর্ম ক্লিয়ার
                document.getElementById('newQuestion').value = '';
                document.getElementById('newAnswer').value = '';
                document.getElementById('newExample').value = '';
                
                alert('নতুন কার্ড যোগ করা হয়েছে!');
            } else {
                alert('প্রশ্ন এবং উত্তর দিন');
            }
        }
        
        filterCards();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৪৮: স্পেলিং চেকার
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>স্পেলিং চেকার</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            max-width: 700px;
            width: 90%;
        }
        h1 {
            text-align: center;
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        
        .input-area {
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        
        textarea {
            width: 100%;
            height: 200px;
            padding: 15px;
            font-size: 16px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 10px;
            box-sizing: border-box;
            resize: vertical;
        }
        
        .stats {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            padding: 15px;
            background: #f9f9f9;
            border-radius: 10px;
        }
        
        .stat-item {
            text-align: center;
        }
        
        .stat-label {
            color: #666;
            font-size: 14px;
        }
        
        .stat-value {
            font-size: 24px;
            font-weight: bold;
            color: #667eea;
        }
        
        .check-btn {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 15px;
            background: #667eea;
            color: white;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 8px;
            cursor: pointer;
            font-size: 18px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        
        .check-btn:hover {
            background: #764ba2;
            transform: translateY(-2px);
            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(102,126,234,0.4);
        }
        
        .result-area {
            background: #f9f9f9;
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 10px;
            max-height: 300px;
            overflow-y: auto;
        }
        
        .result-title {
            font-size: 18px;
            font-weight: bold;
            margin-bottom: 15px;
            color: #333;
        }
        
        .word-item {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            align-items: center;
            padding: 10px;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #e0e0e0;
        }
        
        .word-item:last-child {
            border-bottom: none;
        }
        
        .word-text {
            font-size: 16px;
        }
        
        .word-text.correct {
            color: #43e97b;
        }
        
        .word-text.incorrect {
            color: #f44336;
        }
        
        .suggestions {
            display: flex;
            gap: 5px;
            flex-wrap: wrap;
        }
        
        .suggestion {
            padding: 5px 10px;
            background: white;
            border: 1px solid #667eea;
            border-radius: 15px;
            font-size: 12px;
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        
        .suggestion:hover {
            background: #667eea;
            color: white;
        }
        
        .add-dictionary {
            margin-top: 20px;
            display: flex;
            gap: 10px;
        }
        
        #newWord {
            flex: 1;
            padding: 10px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 5px;
        }
        
        .add-btn {
            padding: 10px 20px;
            background: #43e97b;
            color: white;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 5px;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
        
        .add-btn:hover {
            background: #38f9d7;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>✓ স্পেলিং চেকার</h1>
        
        <div class="input-area">
            <textarea id="textInput" placeholder="আপনার টেক্সট লিখুন..."></textarea>
        </div>
        
        <div class="stats">
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-label">মোট শব্দ</div>
                <div class="stat-value" id="totalWords">0</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-label">সঠিক</div>
                <div class="stat-value" id="correctWords">0</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-item">
                <div class="stat-label">ভুল</div>
                <div class="stat-value" id="incorrectWords">0</div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <button class="check-btn" onclick="checkSpelling()">স্পেলিং চেক করুন</button>
        
        <div class="result-area" id="result">
            <div class="result-title">ফলাফল</div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="add-dictionary">
            <input type="text" id="newWord" placeholder="নতুন শব্দ যোগ করুন">
            <button class="add-btn" onclick="addToDictionary()">ডিকশনারিতে যোগ করুন</button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // সিম্পল ডিকশনারি
        let dictionary = [
            'the', 'be', 'to', 'of', 'and', 'a', 'in', 'that', 'have', 'i',
            'it', 'for', 'not', 'on', 'with', 'he', 'as', 'you', 'do', 'at',
            'this', 'but', 'his', 'by', 'from', 'they', 'we', 'say', 'her', 'she',
            'or', 'an', 'will', 'my', 'one', 'all', 'would', 'there', 'their',
            'what', 'so', 'up', 'out', 'if', 'about', 'who', 'get', 'which', 'go',
            'me', 'when', 'make', 'can', 'like', 'time', 'no', 'just', 'him', 'know',
            'take', 'person', 'into', 'year', 'your', 'good', 'some', 'could', 'them',
            'see', 'other', 'than', 'then', 'now', 'look', 'only', 'come', 'its', 'over',
            'think', 'also', 'back', 'after', 'use', 'two', 'how', 'our', 'work',
            'first', 'well', 'way', 'even', 'new', 'want', 'because', 'any', 'these',
            'give', 'day', 'most', 'us'
        ];
        
        function checkSpelling() {
            const text = document.getElementById('textInput').value;
            const words = text.toLowerCase().match(/\b\w+\b/g) || [];
            
            const totalWords = words.length;
            let correctCount = 0;
            let incorrectWords = [];
            
            const resultDiv = document.getElementById('result');
            resultDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="result-title">ফলাফল</div>';
            
            words.forEach(word => {
                const isCorrect = dictionary.includes(word);
                if (isCorrect) {
                    correctCount++;
                } else {
                    incorrectWords.push(word);
                }
                
                const wordDiv = document.createElement('div');
                wordDiv.className = 'word-item';
                wordDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <span class="word-text ${isCorrect ? 'correct' : 'incorrect'}">${word}</span>
                    ${!isCorrect ? getSuggestions(word) : ''}
                `;
                resultDiv.appendChild(wordDiv);
            });
            
            document.getElementById('totalWords').textContent = totalWords;
            document.getElementById('correctWords').textContent = correctCount;
            document.getElementById('incorrectWords').textContent = totalWords - correctCount;
        }
        
        function getSuggestions(word) {
            const suggestions = findSuggestions(word);
            if (suggestions.length > 0) {
                return `
                    <div class="suggestions">
                        ${suggestions.map(s => `<span class="suggestion" onclick="useSuggestion('${s}')">${s}</span>`).join('')}
                    </div>
                `;
            }
            return '';
        }
        
        function findSuggestions(word) {
            const suggestions = [];
            
            // ১ অক্ষরের পার্থক্য
            for (const dictWord of dictionary) {
                if (Math.abs(dictWord.length - word.length) <= 2) {
                    if (levenshteinDistance(word, dictWord) <= 2) {
                        suggestions.push(dictWord);
                    }
                }
            }
            
            return suggestions.slice(0, 5);
        }
        
        function levenshteinDistance(a, b) {
            const matrix = [];
            
            for (let i = 0; i <= b.length; i++) {
                matrix[i] = [i];
            }
            
            for (let j = 0; j <= a.length; j++) {
                matrix[0][j] = j;
            }
            
            for (let i = 1; i <= b.length; i++) {
                for (let j = 1; j <= a.length; j++) {
                    if (b.charAt(i - 1) === a.charAt(j - 1)) {
                        matrix[i][j] = matrix[i - 1][j - 1];
                    } else {
                        matrix[i][j] = Math.min(
                            matrix[i - 1][j - 1] + 1,
                            matrix[i][j - 1] + 1,
                            matrix[i - 1][j] + 1
                        );
                    }
                }
            }
            
            return matrix[b.length][a.length];
        }
        
        function useSuggestion(word) {
            alert(`'${word}' শব্দটি ব্যবহার করুন`);
        }
        
        function addToDictionary() {
            const newWord = document.getElementById('newWord').value.toLowerCase().trim();
            if (newWord && !dictionary.includes(newWord)) {
                dictionary.push(newWord);
                document.getElementById('newWord').value = '';
                alert(`'${newWord}' ডিকশনারিতে যোগ করা হয়েছে!`);
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>
প্রজেক্ট ৪৯: অ্যানাগ্রাম চেকার
html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>অ্যানাগ্রাম চেকার</title>
    <style>
        body {
            font-family: 'Arial', sans-serif;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f093fb 0%, #f5576c 100%);
            min-height: 100vh;
            margin: 0;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
        }
        .container {
            background: white;
            padding: 40px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
            max-width: 600px;
            width: 90%;
        }
        h1 {
            text-align: center;
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
        }
        
        .input-group {
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        
        label {
            display: block;
            margin-bottom: 5px;
            color: #666;
            font-weight: bold;
        }
        
        input {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 12px;
            font-size: 16px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 8px;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }
        
        .check-btn {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 15px;
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, #f093fb 0%, #f5576c 100%);
            color: white;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 8px;
            cursor: pointer;
            font-size: 18px;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
            transition: all 0.3s;
        }
        
        .check-btn:hover {
            transform: translateY(-2px);
            box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(240,147,251,0.4);
        }
        
        .result {
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 10px;
            text-align: center;
            margin-bottom: 30px;
            display: none;
        }
        
        .result.anagram {
            background: #d4edda;
            color: #155724;
            display: block;
        }
        
        .result.not-anagram {
            background: #f8d7da;
            color: #721c24;
            display: block;
        }
        
        .anagram-list {
            background: #f9f9f9;
            padding: 20px;
            border-radius: 10px;
        }
        
        .anagram-list h3 {
            color: #333;
            margin-bottom: 15px;
        }
        
        .anagram-item {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: space-between;
            padding: 10px;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #e0e0e0;
        }
        
        .anagram-item:last-child {
            border-bottom: none;
        }
        
        .word-pair {
            display: flex;
            gap: 20px;
        }
        
        .word {
            font-weight: bold;
        }
        
        .status {
            color: #f5576c;
        }
        
        .find-more {
            margin-top: 20px;
        }
        
        #findWord {
            width: 70%;
            padding: 10px;
            border: 2px solid #e0e0e0;
            border-radius: 5px 0 0 5px;
        }
        
        .find-btn {
            padding: 10px 20px;
            background: #f5576c;
            color: white;
            border: none;
            border-radius: 0 5px 5px 0;
            cursor: pointer;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <h1>🔄 অ্যানাগ্রাম চেকার</h1>
        
        <div class="input-group">
            <label>প্রথম শব্দ:</label>
            <input type="text" id="word1" placeholder="যেমন: listen">
        </div>
        
        <div class="input-group">
            <label>দ্বিতীয় শব্দ:</label>
            <input type="text" id="word2" placeholder="যেমন: silent">
        </div>
        
        <button class="check-btn" onclick="checkAnagram()">পরীক্ষা করুন</button>
        
        <div class="result" id="result"></div>
        
        <div class="anagram-list">
            <h3>উদাহরণ অ্যানাগ্রাম</h3>
            <div id="exampleAnagrams"></div>
            
            <div class="find-more">
                <h3>অ্যানাগ্রাম খুঁজুন</h3>
                <input type="text" id="findWord" placeholder="শব্দ লিখুন">
                <button class="find-btn" onclick="findAnagrams()">খুঁজুন</button>
                <div id="foundAnagrams"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const exampleAnagrams = [
            ['listen', 'silent'],
            ['angel', 'glean'],
            ['earth', 'heart'],
            ['night', 'thing'],
            ['astronomer', 'moon starer'],
            ['debit card', 'bad credit'],
            ['school master', 'the classroom'],
            ['conversation', 'voices rant on'],
            ['eleven plus two', 'twelve plus one'],
            ['the eyes', 'they see']
        ];
        
        function displayExamples() {
            const container = document.getElementById('exampleAnagrams');
            container.innerHTML = exampleAnagrams.map(pair => `
                <div class="anagram-item">
                    <div class="word-pair">
                        <span class="word">${pair[0]}</span>
                        <span>⇄</span>
                        <span class="word">${pair[1]}</span>
                    </div>
                    <span class="status">✓ অ্যানাগ্রাম</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        }
        
        function checkAnagram() {
            const word1 = document.getElementById('word1').value;
            const word2 = document.getElementById('word2').value;
            const resultDiv = document.getElementById('result');
            
            if (!word1 || !word2) {
                alert('দয়া করে দুটি শব্দ লিখুন');
                return;
            }
            
            const cleaned1 = word1.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '').split('').sort().join('');
            const cleaned2 = word2.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '').split('').sort().join('');
            
            const isAnagram = cleaned1 === cleaned2 && cleaned1 !== '';
            
            if (isAnagram) {
                resultDiv.className = 'result anagram';
                resultDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <strong>অভিনন্দন!</strong> "${word1}" এবং "${word2}" অ্যানাগ্রাম!
                `;
            } else {
                resultDiv.className = 'result not-anagram';
                resultDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <strong>দুঃখিত!</strong> "${word1}" এবং "${word2}" অ্যানাগ্রাম নয়।
                `;
            }
        }
        
        function findAnagrams() {
            const word = document.getElementById('findWord').value;
            const foundDiv = document.getElementById('foundAnagrams');
            
            if (!word) {
                alert('একটি শব্দ লিখুন');
                return;
            }
            
            const cleaned = word.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, '').split('').sort().join('');
            const found = [];
            
            // কিছু কমন শব্দ থেকে খুঁজি
            const commonWords = [
                'silent', 'listen', 'angel', 'glean', 'earth', 'heart',
                'night', 'thing', 'aster', 'stare', 'rates', 'tears',
                'dear', 'read', 'dare', 'fired', 'fried', 'cried',
                'icier', 'melon', 'lemon', 'stone', 'tones', 'notes'
            ];
            
            for (const w of commonWords) {
                const wCleaned = w.split('').sort().join('');
                if (wCleaned === cleaned && w !== word.toLowerCase()) {
                    found.push(w);
                }
            }
            
            if (found.length > 0) {
                foundDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <h4>পাওয়া গেছে:</h4>
                    ${found.map(w => `<span class="suggestion" onclick="useWord('${w}')">${w}</span>`).join(' ')}
                `;
            } else {
                foundDiv.innerHTML = '<p>কোনো অ্যানাগ্রাম পাওয়া যায়নি</p>';
            }
        }
        
        function useWord(word) {
            document.getElementById('word2').value = word;
            checkAnagram();
        }
        
        displayExamples();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
